Two flew over, then circled, and were joined by three or more others.  We walked down the airstrip and I saw birds in the top of a tree.  At first I did not know they were these birds.  Then one flew into a hole in a thinnish-trunked tree.  Another joined it on the trunk of the same tree and later flew away. Then the first bird poked about halfway out of the treehole.  It was late, and hard to see details on the bird.  Looking carefully I could make out the white bare area on its face - no chestnut front.  It then became clear that these were the same Red-bellied Macaws that flew over earlier.  Dan took pictures - the features were easier to see in the photos.	obs185188	Joanie	Patterson	S5042152	eBird - Casual Observation	EBIRD					1		1	0
